almost all video or audio codecs that may exist, so you will not worry about the media file types. It plays everything! \r\nSpecial Effects can be added during the playback, making your videos really exciting! The most advanced is to watch the normal (2D) video in 3D mode (with anaglyph glasses). Totally, 16 unique effects are supported! \r\nmyPlayer 3D+ have also some advanced Video Editing capabilities:\r\n1) You can Create new Videos from an existing one, and add one of the Real Time Video Effects (make them 3D from 2D, Cartoon, Lomogaphic, Vignette, Old Movie, Halftone etc), add background music, trim the duration, adjust the brigthness, contrast, resolution or the video codec.\r\n2) You can create a new video from your personal photos and add into it all the above characteristics (effects, mixing music, brigthness, saturation, contrast, the video resolution or even the video codec\r\n3) You can merge multiple videos of any kind of format (mp4, mkv, flv, etc) and create a new one using the same video resolution and format.\r\n\r\nYou can also Create Playlists from your favorite’s media by combining videos and music from your collections together in the same list. \r\nFinally, you are also able to download to your PC every video that is stored elsewhere (OneDrive. Google Drive, DropBox, Web), or upload every local video to your OneDrive. \r\nAs far as we know there isn’t such application exist in no platform, so we are very proud to bring it for the first time to Windows Store!
